# <a name="obsolete-members-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="635a8-102">.NET Framework에서 사용되지 않는 멤버</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="635a8-102">Obsolete Members in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="635a8-103">이 문서의 표에는 .NET Framework 4.5 이상 버전에서 사용되지 않은 형식 멤버가 어셈블리별로 구성되어 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="635a8-103">The tables in this article list the type members that are obsolete in the .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="635a8-104">각 어셈블리에서 사용되지 않는 멤버 목록과 권장되는 대체 항목을 확인하려면 다음 링크를 사용합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="635a8-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete members and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="635a8-105">사용되지 않는 형식의 멤버는 이 항목에 나열되지 않습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="635a8-105">This topic doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="635a8-106">사용되지 않는 형식 목록은 [사용되지 않는 형식](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-types.md)을 참조하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="635a8-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete Types](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-types.md).</span></span>

<a name="SystemMembers"></a>   
## <a name="obsolete-members-in-system-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="635a8-140">시스템 어셈블리에서 사용되지 않는 멤버</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="635a8-140">Obsolete Members in System Assemblies</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="635a8-141">다음 표에서는 시스템 어셈블리에서 사용되지 않는 멤버를 보여 줍니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="635a8-141">The following tables list the obsolete members in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="635a8-142">이러한 어셈블리는 .NET Framework를 대상으로 하는 일반\-용도의 응용 프로그램 개발에 사용됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="635a8-142">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>  
  
<a name="mscorlib"></a>

## <a name="obsolete-members-in-microsoft-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="635a8-1139">Microsoft 어셈블리에서 사용되지 않는 멤버</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="635a8-1139">Obsolete Members in Microsoft Assemblies</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="635a8-1140">다음 표에서는 Microsoft 어셈블리에서 사용되지 않는 멤버를 보여 줍니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="635a8-1140">The following tables list the obsolete members in Microsoft assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="635a8-1141">특수한 용도의 어셈블리로, 개별 언어(예: Microsoft.VisualBasic.dll) 또는 빌드 시스템(예: Microsoft.Build.Engine.dll)을 대상으로 하는 어셈블리를 포함합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="635a8-1141">These are special-purpose assemblies and include assemblies that target an individual language (such as Microsoft.VisualBasic.dll) or a build system (such as Microsoft.Build.Engine.dll).</span></span>  
  
<a name="IEHost"></a>   
### <a name="assembly-iehostdll-and-ieexecexe"></a><span data-ttu-id="635a8-1142">어셈블리: IEHost.dll 및 IEExec.exe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="635a8-1142">Assembly: IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="635a8-1143">IEHost.dll 및 IEExec.exe 어셈블리는 .NET Framework에서 제거되었습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="635a8-1143">The IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe assemblies have been removed from the .NET Framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="635a8-1144">해당 형식 및 멤버는 모두 사용되지 않으며 [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)]에서 지원되지 않습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="635a8-1144">All of their types and their members are obsolete and are not supported in the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)].</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="635a8-1145">이러한 어셈블리는 Windows Forms 컨트롤을 호스팅하여 Internet Explorer에서 실행 파일을 실행하기 위해 사용되었습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="635a8-1145">These assemblies were used to host Windows Forms controls and to run executables in Internet Explorer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="635a8-1146">이 기술의 대안으로 ClickOnce, XBAP(XAML 브라우저 응용 프로그램) 및 Microsoft Silverlight가 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="635a8-1146">Alternatives to this technology include ClickOnce, XAML Browser Applications (XBAP), and Microsoft Silverlight.</span></span>
